af:["$","p",null,{"children":"Claude Code's cold start optimization isn't a single silver bullet but a combination of carefully designed techniques:"}]
b0:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Parallel prefetching"}]," hides async I/O behind synchronous module evaluation"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Compile-time dead code elimination"}]," removes unused feature module trees at build time"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Dynamic import() lazy loading"}]," defers the cost of heavy modules until first use"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"The profileCheckpoint() profiling system"}]," provides zero-overhead performance observability"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"The deferred require pattern"}]," solves circular dependencies with minimal invasiveness"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mode-aware fast paths"}]," skip unnecessary initialization based on the usage scenario"]}],"\n"]}]
